The Data Of Retail

 

 

On Friday, Google acquired Rangespan, the second UK company Google has bought this year. Based in London, the company provides back-office services for online retail, with a focus on expanding product selection. Sounds like something Amazon does, no? Rangespan has raised $5 million, and will shut down operations to integrate with Google. Rangespan said on its home page, "As part of the change, we will wind down Rangespan's services. We've already begun working individually with each of our retailers and suppliers on this process." Read more via TechCrunch <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001_-Rn4Unw1rNG4zvGuouor8o6j8dHVw_MnanScnm9PhouIGyKZbv_I7dIWjZhO5j3PMHxSdVa3ow3irvRQxxix2PLblVqi499XqATlk2odD3WCNU1zhQ01zAxjkyB6mM8SHuYF6Zn-xchaveqKNMcR8WBOh4o0u9rXl3d0q4d8xPvtNSclJUITzw883P3OfXzjzooQ45kNilTJeEosO0PhPhV91tN_Wwt5IzlwTL0NGguO15_L95Ip7bkf2yt2R4wEpv7P1EOuElpwDoQLmdkXYcvpydym2HoKlM2qSOjkTiKWqBq3Yc-CV6p3fswy5eK&c=v4tZr_HIiYaRCJCnngEPFXShVLaFoBrPNYjmnMX5G2HkkRJ2781itQ==&ch=_Nfm87XznXOHTyXZYaIG-MaYmrL6tyh1D2L5euYljXJG-_NCWiedeg==> . 

 

The Native Lag 

 

Big publishers such as BuzzFeed, Business Insider and HuffPost are increasingly expanding ad operations abroad, yet ad revenue has been slow to follow. Digiday reports, "Overseas, publishers are finding that display still dominates. The native ad craze that's sweeping through the U.S. hasn't caught on overseas." This could prove to be a challenge for publishers like BuzzFeed, whose ad strategy follows a native-only model. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001_-Rn4Unw1rNG4zvGuouor8o6j8dHVw_MnanScnm9PhouIGyKZbv_I7dIWjZhO5j3xZL842TmNQjUzvOK0H3ieLRzBOmlXdkUIvQPubCOOfmrvcuHMQhERZ0zAQIsun08RWTQOG1JDyljG_Y6mJ57ktn9Giy9_tRYdUNcH74fdM110kgWsAYXiQZHz4YcN9u-JaR2PH5Mk4iV6dD_yL7gK88sghj6WzfT5wKBzkhvCwov26rTYeLjieMf4S1AngVzwPJC4KiJf9A=&c=v4tZr_HIiYaRCJCnngEPFXShVLaFoBrPNYjmnMX5G2HkkRJ2781itQ==&ch=_Nfm87XznXOHTyXZYaIG-MaYmrL6tyh1D2L5euYljXJG-_NCWiedeg==> . 

 

Harnessing Enterprise Data 

 

HootSuite has unveiled its latest social SaaS platform, "uberVUBoards," and the company's analytics GM, Mark Pascarelo, calls it the first step to "democratizing social media." The platform is a data-visualization tool, which lets users identify a metric, pin it to a dashboard and generate a report. The widget was designed with HR specialists, IT crews and investor relations in mind, and seeks to address the increasing uses for social media data. Read more via PandoDaily <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001_-Rn4Unw1rNG4zvGuouor8o6j8dHVw_MnanScnm9PhouIGyKZbv_I7dIWjZhO5j3d3h7_aW9aLjhGDvNTJH-dLDtoXjL5s-N861mepR2274MmsdJgOClDbjW-7XImyNCHa5BRLN58h0wIGh6iIMMtLcmRnh3dS7xkEaSM8-qpz9pTEfUIcsd1jroeOaBFtp3Ne24tXnDLIt7SbMXA8lsdQ8dUWs_chn3lVPG0bucfNybbfgFMxAAtN2bjzhEQS0ssjnnVCLOcrCxdYEmcw0waai8qX6XOOzk&c=v4tZr_HIiYaRCJCnngEPFXShVLaFoBrPNYjmnMX5G2HkkRJ2781itQ==&ch=_Nfm87XznXOHTyXZYaIG-MaYmrL6tyh1D2L5euYljXJG-_NCWiedeg==> . Enterprise data will and does meet marketing data. 

 

Addressing TV "Tribes" 

 

You could say Time Warner Cable Media is quietly disassociating itself from television to stick with the cross-screen script. The ad sales side of the cable conglomerate took a device-agnostic approach to its digital NewFront on Friday, launching "Audience Select," a cross-screen audience-targeting tool. It also debuted in-house creative agency Kernel to help marketers plan multiscreen campaigns that tap in to TWC's anonymized audience data set, dubbed "TV Tribes." More onCNBC <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001_-Rn4Unw1rNG4zvGuouor8o6j8dHVw_MnanScnm9PhouIGyKZbv_I7dIWjZhO5j3FEiqJKtZC8AyDwKM2ow8nnzoIQ0t7_vqrW1rddEar_G6wkgc5OVtl_ExXvtziqfV06ca74fxfbCHmZz-SBU3A-EJ4gkjUbGwLK52ki3viAYBkfusUSY_y8kfz0PTcJeG&c=v4tZr_HIiYaRCJCnngEPFXShVLaFoBrPNYjmnMX5G2HkkRJ2781itQ==&ch=_Nfm87XznXOHTyXZYaIG-MaYmrL6tyh1D2L5euYljXJG-_NCWiedeg==> .

 

The Big Win 

 

Earlier this year, four holding companies pitched Microsoft for control of its global and media ad business and on Friday Dentsu and IPG emerged victorious over Publicis and WPP. The shift is part of Microsoft's ongoing efforts to centralize marketing, a concept the company is calling "One Microsoft." IPG will take charge of creative efforts worldwide, whereas Dentsu will manage Microsoft's media planning and buying, as well as search ads overseas. ClickZ has the story <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001_-Rn4Unw1rNG4zvGuouor8o6j8dHVw_MnanScnm9PhouIGyKZbv_I7dIWjZhO5j3-r5Ew5aBkrV3uq6vrQMDkNN9qKWWamZUHFG17d6t4xVKVbXnesTC0mnefIZazO_J-WDsRsm2BekIV59m-wTQQjQK5xMJP839C0h3FCDJs9cLy61FioX_SbXcx8cjYGs91PL1d3_4jCDrhUZC3K8lWhpYyFYSBBiLDYn6f2a7YjviLDh8N6PTToruKk_nZRvi3kKyyu1qAAjVgWJpVXGdNg==&c=v4tZr_HIiYaRCJCnngEPFXShVLaFoBrPNYjmnMX5G2HkkRJ2781itQ==&ch=_Nfm87XznXOHTyXZYaIG-MaYmrL6tyh1D2L5euYljXJG-_NCWiedeg==> . This would seem to be good news for the Dentsu-Aegis trading desk AMNET.

Foursquare Transforms


Location-sharing app Foursquare is splitting in two. The "check-in" function that defined it from day one will be rebranded as Swarm <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001eBI6EpKOqmvJpVb7Lb92dYoR_rfinpqlysWTEMZ-KF3RxUdBDvLo_RA43WvsDcJeZSOGnqIyk8Iu9jgjMoXF5aVYth6gR5xzUvtucaH8ox_8q_J5lPTL4v2Y0C57bttVtwHafvCaa0TSLWimpCM3HDezX_sJEFFlRtU_UyK2Hdo=&c=AQMfIw0UT7AQvANg3X-0q4miQPyQW3KgZbmI6_YHJQbHgo5G3xeG-Q==&ch=u2xH2EwoZu4hlB9Y8_aAEwniI2vvdqAV9GxwG3V6wfAqxM09wPFGXA==> . Meanwhile a rewritten version of Foursquare will support search and discovery. Foursquare's VP of product experience, Jon Steinback, said, "Mobile forced this fundamental switch. We were born in mobile but we were born in this idea that each mobile app was kind of like a Web property bundled up for mobile." The Verge has the story <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001eBI6EpKOqmvJpVb7Lb92dYoR_rfinpqlysWTEMZ-KF3RxUdBDvLo_RA43WvsDcJeQQrm4w_m86SV0zwWc--fN299zz8MLVwWRomT5AugoE8Obu20HG6n4gmOvJBeuSjCpC-9b6WKRnHUXYUXt_Le3oUSpbNmiFobGSCuWXYJ9KXUClSUEs-OJ7g3okd6w4weprhMx23BW6aRtDSqos2AFJgyE91mn6SSb3SrYrnG5_s=&c=AQMfIw0UT7AQvANg3X-0q4miQPyQW3KgZbmI6_YHJQbHgo5G3xeG-Q==&ch=u2xH2EwoZu4hlB9Y8_aAEwniI2vvdqAV9GxwG3V6wfAqxM09wPFGXA==> . Services On Top


Yext has decided to add a professional service team to its SaaS offerings with the purchase of Citrrus - its first acquisition. So says Yext CEO Howard Lerman, who tells TechCrunch that "getting the product to work for enterprise customers can require more customization." Hence, the acqui-hire of sorts. Instagram's Video Ads


ClickZ's sources say Instagram is testing sponsored video ads with advertising partners, and has not yet confirmed a specific launch date. Adweek reports <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001eBI6EpKOqmvJpVb7Lb92dYoR_rfinpqlysWTEMZ-KF3RxUdBDvLo_RA43WvsDcJeJ8jUcGNtnm6KKAOaQrseeqSziXiHT4SXbh9dARNJbBhTY5yFX3gG7Mf2zdbQ9Mro-iajSc7YLxByitU9uG7V5rr6axSuOYP2CBm8V3kwu_BMdb6FDpLwhyGqVj7yCqFy8YbF9ZBSYl_eqU2AU30u87yNCXrDzvsvdES5TT-tVlHrKCw5frwTeJTW7sNbroZ2&c=AQMfIw0UT7AQvANg3X-0q4miQPyQW3KgZbmI6_YHJQbHgo5G3xeG-Q==&ch=u2xH2EwoZu4hlB9Y8_aAEwniI2vvdqAV9GxwG3V6wfAqxM09wPFGXA==>  that Instagram's early advertising partners include Burberry, Ben & Jerry's and Levi's. Chaney Marketing Group founder Paul Chaney comments, "In my experience, Facebook's standard operating procedure is to test with a small sample, then roll out changes on a broader scale. I wouldn't be surprised if that wasn't the case with Instagram as well." The White House On Big Data


On Thursday, the White House released a highly anticipated report that details the tech industry's collection of big data and how it affects the online privacy of Americans. In a parallel report from the President's Council of Advisors on Science and Technology, co-chair John Holdren writes, "In light of the continuing proliferation of ways to collect and use information about people, PCAST recommends that policy focus primarily on whether specific uses of information about people affect privacy adversely. It also recommends that policy focus on outcomes, on the 'what' rather than the 'how,' to avoid becoming obsolete as technology advances." Read The Washington Post <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001eBI6EpKOqmvJpVb7Lb92dYoR_rfinpqlysWTEMZ-KF3RxUdBDvLo_RA43WvsDcJeS6ZJ-ig1ZZwNfnemTG77clGg7tI_c3ZQoiAgcyt5ra5wprTE__f_2HbOU1a1zH8FOzucE5VkgsE8uUrosulDMte3fw3eANxrnC8kqUxISa-i88IddqlvYqC5qCiMuoAlLYKQHZodmlxTAVe3BXzkSE1Y-GBz6fpiOKwxHhRkd0JiBdSMa30SJUEqsRnl92P8WSWyJLFYVzbKikdkMfg13i-LTcuRCRuxco9empkEiOYHG_cMA2vV-Q==&c=AQMfIw0UT7AQvANg3X-0q4miQPyQW3KgZbmI6_YHJQbHgo5G3xeG-Q==&ch=u2xH2EwoZu4hlB9Y8_aAEwniI2vvdqAV9GxwG3V6wfAqxM09wPFGXA==> . 


The Rise Of Tablets


Tablets are becoming more important for advertising and ecommerce, according to an eMarketer report released Thursday. Findings detail that consumers use of tablets will grow an estimated 11.3%, reaching 147.2 million users this year. "Despite the growth of mobile video viewing and the relative stagnation of video viewing on PCs, ad spending still skews heavily toward online video. ... [I]nvestments in online video ads in the US will reach $4.45 billion this year, dwarfing mobile video ad spending, which will total $1.44 billion." Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001eBI6EpKOqmvJpVb7Lb92dYoR_rfinpqlysWTEMZ-KF3RxUdBDvLo_RA43WvsDcJe23WSySZRRSRqOpJAK-6TG1AtC865ICNPLq9wT7dAcWSnR-BfYqL5VA0MUWuPrehvJrkw6MQpMQ4hZnZ_Y1Ol-Isox-llaj70N8cKo_Hb5agfI5d1g_EnOhgh2T52HnVLLMyTRkxtYWrPn0h_ZCgZXQ2BW35UD8dMOVczm08K-rtgLSka-rji8zWXTEGi-VttrWGRNs4MAfX43FS4vV2wgw==&c=AQMfIw0UT7AQvANg3X-0q4miQPyQW3KgZbmI6_YHJQbHgo5G3xeG-Q==&ch=u2xH2EwoZu4hlB9Y8_aAEwniI2vvdqAV9GxwG3V6wfAqxM09wPFGXA==> . 


Pardot's Popular For Programmatic


VentureBeat reports that the fastest-growing marketing automation system is Pardot, Salesforce's subsidiary. According to the stats, Pardot is gaining customers faster than Hubspot, Marketo, Act-On or DemandForce. Although Pardot has steadily been raking in new clients at a rate of 200-400 monthly, the data from April saw Pardot's new client figure swell to 1,128. Marketo, for comparison, gained 518 new clients that same month. Get the full story <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=001eBI6EpKOqmvJpVb7Lb92dYoR_rfinpqlysWTEMZ-KF3RxUdBDvLo_RA43WvsDcJeQV5j-7AVxWexgUDCbhnr1st8r9qiQegyrNfODRfS6ckvdmqwQurxQQOwN9Saf75CJiofHhLLtwKsPnwaDGjtz1k3Fi53XsTWKDDD7iUMXq0JszxEJGlGKX3ZDEAdlAiA1iZeWzGB679frXfYJk89naOA4hSGx-LAWb7zsIu2DiwNZc4Avw2bfIXHrx_aBUPOEhimevtQVLOVK2ojy43EbeyFEVHtexhCHDimjbM7RpmOZoJSjW49RcXRo657lUqf&c=AQMfIw0UT7AQvANg3X-0q4miQPyQW3KgZbmI6_YHJQbHgo5G3xeG-Q==&ch=u2xH2EwoZu4hlB9Y8_aAEwniI2vvdqAV9GxwG3V6wfAqxM09wPFGXA==> .

Dating Native Ads


The free dating app Tinder <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=0011uWUDLfUQhydcd1Z0xNMY61xbebj_O5UT8gNzZDFsb3YpddcdqICwP_Xec2flMtkwM5SrkCS1jz2zKkTfc93vOgClUUT098QbB3r2M_XAKD5HVQ6bTwbqMUmDv_xk3RExx2g64qW5uAIRGi4ERxnkHfte3NwlnSU3AqA9ImlHW0=&c=qFutfDDF-cmWTWOfDVWPKgh7eoCp6FVqcBvMSheNbzviOFD39FMJeg==&ch=WmDjVZYij1iHo_HnzA3kZ522C_7cTBpuy8GcxU5e9Am5ii6ix8CCFQ==> , owned in part by IAC, will eventually feature ads, executives said on an earnings call. One option, according to IAC's Greg Blatt, would be native advertising. As Re/code's Peter Kafka reports, two networks have already experimented with running campaigns on Tinder through the use of fake dating profiles for the shows' characters, but no money was made. Read the rest <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=0011uWUDLfUQhydcd1Z0xNMY61xbebj_O5UT8gNzZDFsb3YpddcdqICwP_Xec2flMtkwVkA8iCZHl3d2dJyrYpLKK1Z8-2Bp1DGWpOzYlqAnk08kslmxkzReUd_ZuFT3o2DaDSaj7r1cb5yxitgHv_vBr0Cbahv1wfyfP2AhkYcwQMvbYOFn7dSouAmhdNPSbZZSUNixtzfgDotHItbd4IgvvqVBGYmJ-gqm42FABVonQLx7VtmGlVtgQ==&c=qFutfDDF-cmWTWOfDVWPKgh7eoCp6FVqcBvMSheNbzviOFD39FMJeg==&ch=WmDjVZYij1iHo_HnzA3kZ522C_7cTBpuy8GcxU5e9Am5ii6ix8CCFQ==> . 


New Acronym


Monetizing video on demand has been a struggler for networks, but BlackArrow is working to solve that problem through use of Nielsen's "On-Demand Commercial Ratings." BlackArrow provides a technology that allows current ads to be inserted into older shows, thus making video on demand more appealing for advertisers. According to the release, Nielsen tested its new ratings product with Comcast in late 2013. Read the release <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=0011uWUDLfUQhydcd1Z0xNMY61xbebj_O5UT8gNzZDFsb3YpddcdqICwP_Xec2flMtkNEEl1FGuzBPWSdYRTbWiy698-XUvsSrNWGahP2wE66WVBwPLi7tKex8t-XkiL6-iH8sXpVDPf_K2BJo4CXmx2zLLp-25fBj-gQXjAyxtWrEpaLJmvcJR-wR1N1p4M1OzJwXUGqAo8mVL1Rt8Wv_qarxoe51Y9H1Ic-uMTho5z_lF1T4yyxCkfVW_gnoKx351oQbdmWOppp-B-J37S10F3EQzhQjmfc30ZiyzHCJJsWjLjjYTd6YpGgq9mNmqaGKG-e-YjiRNsOE=&c=qFutfDDF-cmWTWOfDVWPKgh7eoCp6FVqcBvMSheNbzviOFD39FMJeg==&ch=WmDjVZYij1iHo_HnzA3kZ522C_7cTBpuy8GcxU5e9Am5ii6ix8CCFQ==> . 


Dinner And A Show


Hulu is serving up a new type of direct-response ad that allows viewers to order pizza while watching videos. This is among many types of interactive ads that advertisers can customize, according to The Wall Street Journal's Jack Marshall, reporting from the Upfront. Hulu is also dropping the subscription requirement to use the service on mobile, opening up yet another revenue stream. Read more <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=0011uWUDLfUQhydcd1Z0xNMY61xbebj_O5UT8gNzZDFsb3YpddcdqICwP_Xec2flMtk6Vb6MIq-nYpiYhDV9i9ugXpCdaf93DHsVSeP2Z2xIYm_UH28TvI2kGkMnsf5eDFN-Gx_Rp1g-mThmTDehFdea8Il5zJOYYrxR223AouRzx6K9dGDoq6NF1zOgkgkheM6BZqRpZqtv35Pr_jWS9CvdkyymI8ScbHvTQy6QKcWdWXwBIKb9KArVA==&c=qFutfDDF-cmWTWOfDVWPKgh7eoCp6FVqcBvMSheNbzviOFD39FMJeg==&ch=WmDjVZYij1iHo_HnzA3kZ522C_7cTBpuy8GcxU5e9Am5ii6ix8CCFQ==> . 


Changing Perspective


Digital is disrupting traditional agency processes, as noted by Doug Weaver, but there is opportunity in the chaos for media agencies, publishers and sellers. Some advice from Weaver: Agencies should stop focusing on "big ideas" and be more nimble, and sellers should focus more on agency connections than RFPs. Read on <http://r20.rs6.net/tn.jsp?f=0011uWUDLfUQhydcd1Z0xNMY61xbebj_O5UT8gNzZDFsb3YpddcdqICwP_Xec2flMtkzysmIhlpS6duXZHK5GvOGIR-dtm7-sY--OUB-XMkAffEXl-Tr6pA0Za8HsQS52zbDOy5m9yUWDftSFt1pImdUgkK5q-COMWvoXnB1NhPT_-1_EAFTRK9Z2FwyKmvBDCh0C6ki9J9d5r5rh94v97DajhlgBrkyfJq&c=qFutfDDF-cmWTWOfDVWPKgh7eoCp6FVqcBvMSheNbzviOFD39FMJeg==&ch=WmDjVZYij1iHo_HnzA3kZ522C_7cTBpuy8GcxU5e9Am5ii6ix8CCFQ==> .
